##Ludwig the German and his sons
#Ludwig the German
90107 = {
	name = "Ludwig"
	dna = 90107_ludwig_the_german
	# AKA: Ludwig 'der Deutsche'
	dynasty = 25061
	martial = 6
	diplomacy = 5
	intrigue = 7
	stewardship = 5
	religion = "catholic"
	culture = franconian
	trait = education_martial_1
	trait = ambitious
	trait = stubborn
	trait = trusting
	sexuality = heterosexual
	father = 90095
	mother = 91002
	10806.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}
	}
	10826.1.1 = {
		set_primary_title_to = title:k_east_francia
	}
	10827.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 7987 #Hemma
		give_nickname = nick_the_german

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_realm_law = crown_authority_0 }
				add_realm_law = crown_authority_1
			}
		}
	}
	10876.1.29 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

#Karlmann of Bavaria
42018 = {
	name = "Karlmann"
	dna = 42018_karlmann
	dynasty = 25061
	martial = 8
	diplomacy = 5
	intrigue = 3
	stewardship = 5
	learning = 8
	religion = "catholic"
	culture = franconian
	trait = education_martial_4
	trait = greedy
	trait = zealous
	trait = humble
	sexuality = heterosexual
	father = 90107 #(Ludwig the German)
	mother = 7987
	10830.1.14 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}	
	}
	10846.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_friend = { reason = friend_generic_history target = character:7987 } #His mother Hemma, he was her favorite
		}
	}
	10850.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_lover = { reason = lover_history target = character:167813 } # Liutswind
			set_relation_rival = { target = character:167812 reason = rival_historical } # Liutswind's brother, Ernst
		}
	}
	10860.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_rival = { target = character:90107 reason = rival_historical }
			add_opinion = {
				target = character:90107 #Karlmann had a "conflictual" relationship with his father
				modifier = hate_opinion
				opinion = -200
			}
		}
	}
	10864.1.1 = {
		set_primary_title_to = title:d_bavaria
	}
	10866.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 167813# Liutswind
	}
	10867.1.1 = {
		contract_disease_effect = { DISEASE = ill TREATMENT_EVENT = yes }
	}
	10880.9.29 = {
		death = yes
	}
}
